Posted by9 months ago

Is Indian society and culture ego and self driven?

￼

AskIndia

Idk why would this question come into my mind but as teenager who doesn't really have that many friends or any friends to interact to, I always have kind of looked at society with two frames. One through the internet YOUTUBE and other sources such as news and newspapers and the other what's happening around me, my family. I wasn't lucky(or maybe lucky) to have a neighborhood. There are literally no resedential houses or apartments near to my house, it's in the middle of a commercial area, and in the middle means the main road. So growing up I either had school kids to interact with, which because of my absolutely terrible ugly dark face, and a bit (or a lot of bullying), and my bellow average marks were the my self esteem never really stood up. I never really had a meaningful conversation with any fucking human being and talking to girls, can't even think about it. Sorry about my useless story, but wanted to tell you this because, my absolutely zero interaction with people didn't push me into this "Indian Culture" and the norms and regulations most Indians follow unconsciously. Me now a somewhat mature teen, was having this question - That is our society is ego driven. It seems to me like, everything(most of the people) do in this country is just show things off to people and get validation from them. it's like the reason for most people's existence. And you don't just these effects from aunties and mums boozing about their kids or kids trying to show off their pencil box and water bottles. I think it can also be seen at a higher scale, to how politicians work and policemen work. The thing that everyone wants is public recognition and validation. And this can be observed everywhere, just look around observe, people try to show off things brands selling you things to show off and countless other things. The thing that confuses me, is to how we became like this as we are now? Cause it can't be just colonisation or poverty because countries like South Korea Japan and Hong Kong have gone through the same. How did we became so social creatures that most of our actions and decisions are based upon opinions of others??? Writing this I think it could be Bollywood movies, I'm not that familiar with the movies before 2012, what do you think that could be a reason???

PepperX [8k]John Cage wanted to experience total silence so he contacted an audio engineer who could allow him to go inside an anechoic chamber. You know, those dark rooms where the ceiling, walls and most of the floor is covered with pointy foam pyramids. He went inside, and the engineer closed the door and a few minutes later, Cage emerged and said, "It wasn"t totally silent in there. I heard some sound." "Was it a deep, thobbing sound and a high, white noise-like sound?" "Why yes!" Cage replied with a slight grin. "The deep sound was the sound of your heart and circulatory system, and the high sound was your nervous system"s background noise." the engineer said.

LinuxGooo [7k]a boat is moving in a 3 dimensional space, Bayesian. So a compass needs to be gimbaled against all 3 axes, its not related to the latitude. What you might mean is the so called "magnetic compensatoin", which has two factors: ship magnetism, and earth magnetism (related to longitude and latitude = position of the ship).
Bayesian [1k]right, and otherwise the compass is automatically balanced when manufactured
LinuxGooo [7k]the course of the ship finally defines the concrete value of "magnetic compensatoin", a correcting parameter we calculate to define the ship course (magnetic course) from the chart / map course.
LinuxGooo [7k]The mounting on the ship itself depends a lot on the ship magnetism. Not every mounting system is adequate. A compass is always adapted individually to each ship. Its veryx expensive to install a compass, as it needs specialists who are allowed to do it. And give the compass on the ship a certificate.
LinuxGooo [7k]Couple of years ago I worked on a 2 masted steel ship, its compass was total worthless. Because of a strike in a thunderstorm, the hull + superstructure (both made of steel) became so extreme magnetized, that no compass could be used. We only navigated with GPS. That was really crazy.

Bayesian [1k]a compass is balanced depending on your latitude
alfalfa [4k]much safer
Khaleesi [-]bring a dragon on board to cook your meats
LinuxGooo [7k]a boat is moving in a 3 dimensional space, Bayesian. So a compass needs to be gimbaled against all 3 axes, its not related to the latitude. What you might mean is the so called "magnetic compensatoin", which has two factors: ship magnetism, and earth magnetism (related to longitude and latitude = position of the ship).
Bayesian [1k]right, and otherwise the compass is automatically balanced when manufactured
LinuxGooo [7k]the course of the ship finally defines the concrete value of "magnetic compensatoin", a correcting parameter we calculate to define the ship course (magnetic course) from the chart / map course.
LinuxGooo [7k]The mounting on the ship itself depends a lot on the ship magnetism. Not every mounting system is adequate. A compass is always adapted individually to each ship. Its veryx expensive to install a compass, as it needs specialists who are allowed to do it. And give the compass on the ship a certificate.
LinuxGooo [7k]Couple of years ago I worked on a 2 masted steel ship, its compass was total worthless. Because of a strike in a thunderstorm, the hull + superstructure (both made of steel) became so extreme magnetized, that no compass could be used. We only navigated with GPS. That was really crazy.

This room is designed for beginners, so that they won"t be beginners for long! Teaching games and game reviews are encouraged here. Just ask!

*** If you don"t have a rank, please put your estimated rank in the game message when creating a game.

If you"re new to the game, learn the basics here before playing your first game: http://www.playgo.to/iwtg/en

Tutors: Some KGS players have volunteered to help beginners/ double-digit kyu players. Ask Sam, OwyheeMud or MicMacAngl for some free, friendly advice on beginning Go.

Broadcast legend Vin Scully dies at 94
MLB.com ^ | 8/2/2022
Posted on 8/3/2022, 9:33:55 AM by Beave Meister

Vin Scully, the Hall of Fame voice of the Dodgers for 67 years, died, the club announced. He was 94.

“We have lost an icon,” said Dodgers president and CEO Stan Kasten. “The Dodgers Vin Scully was one of the greatest voices in all of sports. He was a giant of a man, not only as a broadcaster, but as a humanitarian. He loved people. He loved life. He loved baseball and the Dodgers. And he loved his family. His voice will always be heard and etched in all of our minds forever. I know he was looking forward to joining the love of his life, Sandi. Our thoughts and prayers go out to his family during this very difficult time. Vin will be truly missed.”

(Excerpt) Read more at mlb.com ...

TOPICS: Chit/Chat
KEYWORDS: baseball; broadcaster; dodgers; goat; humanitarian; mlb; scully; vin; vinscully; voice
He was an Icon for major league baseball. What a class act. Rest well Mr. Scully, rest well...
